Local Supplement

Commentary

Trotsky's Nepotism 143

— Wu

In 1924, Trotsky, in his article "Lessons of the October Revolution," boldly and thoroughly attacked his brother-in-law, Zinoviev, a member of the Central Executive Committee. Of course, this was a so-called "political struggle." As for who was right and who was wrong, we outsiders naturally need not interfere. However, Trotsky, for the sake of his "politics," broke with personal feelings and did not consider his "sister" at all. It is truly worthy of our great surprise. Why is "the political relationship of the country" more important to him than his own "nepotism"?

Foreigners value reason over emotion, while Chinese people value emotion over reason. This is a major difference. "Without someone in the court, don't become an official" has become an aphorism for getting by in the world. So, whoever is "successful in their official career" and becomes a high official, then his brothers-in-law, his in-laws, and whatever else he has, will not have to worry about not having food to eat or not having an official position. The so-called "one person becomes an official, and ten thousand people enjoy the blessings," goes without saying. Everyone with "nepotistic ties" to this high official ascends to heaven like chickens and dogs, and celebrates with their caps. Then, outside of the big "nepotistic relationship," there are small "nepotistic relationships." Outside of the small "nepotistic relationships," there are even smaller "nepotistic relationships." In the meantime, directly and indirectly, implicated and affected, to the point where it is impossible to investigate completely. Such officials can be called "nepotistic officials," which becomes a common practice and infects the whole country, called "a country of nepotism."

This point, in terms of the opportunity for nepotism, in addition to this, there are special rights of nepotistic relationships, and it may be useful to briefly list one or two. Engaging in evil, committing crimes, being greedy and perverting the law, are beyond the reach of national law, first. Once the power and position are high, there are naturally many followers. A centipede, even dead, does not fall down, second. Foreign houses, giant mansions, and luxurious residences are connected to the clouds, and beautiful concubines and delicate wives compete to show off, third. Reason can sometimes indeed overcome emotion, but on this point, emotion can indeed overcome reason.

Therefore, it is inevitable that Trotsky, due to political conflict, thoroughly attacked his brother-in-law, which is too unsympathetic. It is inevitable that Zinoviev was too unwise to be attacked by Trotsky due to political conflict.

Alas! The Russian people are truly fools.

Popular Science

Electric Fence 146

— Xuan

Speaking of electric fences, most people think they are a terrifying thing. In fact, electric fences are not as scary as most people imagine; their efficiency is very low. To know the usefulness of electric fences, 90% is in the fence, and 10% is in the electricity; because breaking the fence is more difficult, but breaking the electricity is very easy.

After the electric fence is energized, the purpose is to cause immediate death when a person touches it, so the voltage used is very high, usually around 3,000 volts (Volt) or more. Because direct current cannot generate such a high voltage, the electricity used in electric fences is alternating current, which is electricity in which the direction of the current changes back and forth within a very short period of time. (Most of the electricity used for electric lights now is this type of electricity.) When no one touches the electric fence, the circuit is not connected. Because the generator used for the electric fence has one end connected to the fence and the other end inserted into the ground, but the fence and the ground are not connected, the circuit cannot be completed. Assuming someone touches the fence, then the circuit between the fence and the ground is connected, and the current flows from the generator to the fence, passes through the human body and into the ground, and then returns from the ground to the generator. The human body loses its life due to the passage of high-voltage current.

The alternating current generator used for the electric fence has a very high voltage, but the current is not very high. Therefore, the coils inside this type of generator cannot withstand the passage of strong currents, otherwise the coils will burn out. Breaking the power supply of the electric fence is to take advantage of this point. The method is very simple: use a metal chain, one end connected to a thick metal rod, insert the rod into the ground, and throw the other end onto the electric fence. Then the circuit between the electric fence and the ground is connected, and the current flows from the fence through the metal chain and rod into the ground. Because the metal chain and rod are much thicker than the wires on the fence, their resistance is also much less than the resistance of the wires on the fence. In other words, for the same conductor, the thicker it is, the easier it is for the current to pass through. Therefore, when electricity passes through the chain and rod, a huge current is generated. This strong current, flowing back to the generator from the ground, will burn out the coils of the generator. So, in this way, not only is the power supply on the electric fence cut off, but the generator is also destroyed. However, ordinary generators are equipped with fuses to prevent the passage of strong currents. These fuses have a certain limit to the maximum amount of current they can pass through. If this limit is exceeded, the fuse will melt due to excessive heat, and the strong current cannot pass through. So, when we use the above method to break the power supply of the electric fence, the generator will not be damaged by us. However, its fuse has been blown by the huge current, so the circuit connected to the generator and the electric fence is broken, and the current cannot flow from the generator to the electric fence. At this time, the electric fence is no different from an ordinary barbed wire fence.

During the Shanghai War, everyone said that Japan used electric fences. In fact, according to reliable sources, Japan did not use electric fences this time. I have already said above that 90% of the usefulness of electric fences is in the fence, so the usefulness of electricity is extremely low! This is because breaking the electricity is too easy. Most ordinary people, seeing barbed wire fences, say they are electric fences. The Japanese see that the people of our country are ignorant, and also spread a lot of electric fence rumors to chill the hearts of our army; in fact, what they used were just some barbed wire fences. This is all because the intelligence of the people of our country is too immature, so they are often deceived by others!

Casual Talk

Saving the Nation with Film 147

— Huang Yingdai

The other day, this journal published an article on saving the nation with dancing. If dancing can save the nation, I think those who perform as models will unify the world. In fact, of course, that is impossible; it was just a humorous and satirical essay.

Recently, Chinese youth, in addition to being infatuated with dancing, the level of film enthusiasm is probably even higher than dancing. But I think saving the nation with dancing is just talk, while film can really save the nation.

In the eyes of most people, film seems to be nothing more than a tool for entertainment. In fact, film itself has its own great value. It is the crystallization of art, and at the same time, it is also a good tool for cultivating the minds of the public. Film is indeed a good propaganda tool. For example, during this Sino-Japanese war in Shanghai, we can capture the atrocities of the Japanese army and the tragic situation of Zhabei on camera and project them onto the screen, so that the Chinese public can witness these films and have them deeply imprinted in their minds, never forgetting our enemies and thinking of ways to take revenge.

Furthermore, the battle achievements of the 19th Route Army, we have captured them in the motion picture camera, not only can we show them to the public, but we can also show them inside the army, so that ordinary Chinese soldiers can break the previously held concept of non-resistance and be able to bravely kill the enemy during times of national crisis. However, in fact, most of the films previously produced by Chinese film companies have mainly aimed to cater to social psychology, such as supernatural, martial arts, love, and other films, which are often enough to intoxicate and corrupt the minds of the audience. These kinds of films are not only insufficient to save the nation, but may even be enough to destroy the nation, and the consequences are very dangerous.

Therefore, the Chinese film industry in the future should quickly realize the responsibility of film, change the previously held concept, and actively promote films containing nationalistic character, so that the general audience can understand the dangerous path of the Chinese nation, and everyone can fight for the nation and strive for the permanent survival of the Chinese nation. Only in this way can the film industry fulfill its responsibilities and complete the mission of saving the nation with film.

14. Pudong Police Station v. Xu Hongfu et al. for Assault (Main Text): Defendants Xu Hongfu, Xu Jimin, and Xu Sun are all found not guilty.

15. Laozha Police Station v. Zhu Hailan for Fraud (Main Text): Zhu Hailan is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of fraud; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment; the related civil lawsuit is to be transferred to the civil court of this court for adjudication.

16. Laozha Police Station v. Tao Yurong for Theft (Main Text): Tao Yurong is sentenced to twenty days of detention for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be returned.

17. Laozha Police Station v. Zhao Ganquan for Theft (Main Text): Zhao Ganquan is sentenced to two months and fifteen days of imprisonment for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be stored in the warehouse.

18. Laozha Police Station v. Tan Liugen for Theft (Main Text): Tan Liugen is sentenced to seven days of detention for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be returned.

19. Laozha Police Station v. Wu Asan for Possession of Opium (Main Text): Wu Asan is fined sixty yuan for the crime of possessing opium; if the fine is not paid, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan; the opium is to be confiscated in its original packaging.

20. Laozha Police Station v. Zhang Mingjin for Possession of Opium (Main Text): Zhang Mingjin is fined fifty yuan for the crime of possessing opium substitutes; if the fine is not paid, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan; one package of red pills is to be confiscated in its original packaging.

21. Laozha Police Station v. Tang Chen for Possession of Opium (Main Text): Tang Chen is fined twenty yuan for the crime of possessing opium; if the fine is not paid, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan; the opium is to be confiscated in its original packaging.

22. Laozha Police Station v. Wang Li for Theft (Main Text): Wang Li is sentenced to five days of detention for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be returned.

23. Laozha Police Station v. Xia Jinsheng for Possession of Opium (Main Text): Xia Jinsheng is fined thirty yuan for the crime of possessing opium; if the fine is not paid, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan; the opium is to be confiscated in its original packaging, with a two-year suspended sentence.

24. General Police Station v. Wang Guilin for Theft (Main Text): Wang Guilin, a repeat offender, is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be returned.

25. Huisi Police Station v. Tao Honggen for Theft (Main Text): Tao Honggen is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be returned.

26. Hongshan Police Station v. Li Ada for Theft (Main Text): Li Ada is sentenced to five days of detention for the crime of theft; the original stolen goods are to be returned.

27. Huisi Police Station v. Hu Jusheng for Theft (Main Text): Hu Jusheng is sentenced to seven days of detention for the crime of theft.

28. Jing'an Temple Police Station v. Gu Yanbiao for Theft (Main Text): Gu Yanbiao is sentenced to ten days of detention for the crime of theft, with a two-year suspended sentence.

29. Hongkou Police Station v. Lin Yijin for Theft (Main Text): Lin Yijin is sentenced to ten days of detention for each of three counts of theft, to be executed as twenty days of detention; the stolen goods are to be returned separately.

30. Laozha Police Station v. Liu Wenxuan for Theft (Main Text): Liu Wenxuan is found not guilty.

31. Yangshupu Police Station v. Hu Zhicheng for Theft (Main Text): Hu Zhicheng is sentenced to seven days of detention for the crime of theft.

32. Yangshupu Police Station v. Lu Ahu for Theft (Main Text): Lu Ahu is sentenced to five days of detention for the crime of theft.

33. General Police Station v. Wu Dehai et al. for Theft (Main Text): Wu Dehai is sentenced to five years of imprisonment for theft as a group of three or more; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Yuan Yifang and Jin Chenglong, repeat offenders for theft as a group of three or more, are each sentenced to three years of imprisonment; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

34. Gordon Road Police Station v. Dong Shaochuan for Opium (Main Text): Dong Shaochuan is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined fifty yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium with the intention of profit. Dong Wang is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for assisting in providing premises for others to smoke opium with the intention of profit, with a two-year suspended sentence. Lan Agen and Zhang Zier are each sentenced to two yuan for smoking opium; if the fine is not paid, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. Four small packages of opium, a small amount of opium ash, two opium pipes, two lamps, and two opium trays are to be confiscated. Zhang Fuzhi and Zhang Zixin are found not guilty.

35. General Police Station v. Chen Agen for Theft (Main Text): Chen Agen, a repeat offender for habitual theft, is sentenced to two years of imprisonment; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

36. General Police Station v. Lu Jinsheng for Theft (Main Text): Lu Jinsheng, a repeat offender for theft, is sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

37. Xinzha Police Station v. Wang Xiaosizi for Theft (Main Text): Wang Xiaosizi is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for the crime of theft; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

38. Xinzha Police Station v. Shang Atai for Robbery (Main Text): Gao Atai is given a reduced sentence of two months of imprisonment for the crime of robbery; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

39. Xinzha Police Station v. Wang Abao for Theft (Main Text): Wang Abao, a repeat offender, is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for the crime of breaking into a residence at night to commit theft; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

40. Gordon Road Police Station v. Zhou Ye et al. for Opium (Main Text): Zhou Ye is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined fifty yuan for providing premises for others to smoke opium with the intention of profit. Hang Zhongrong is sentenced to three months of imprisonment and fined thirty yuan for smoking opium. Fan Yinhe, Guan Xiaoting, Wang Genbao, Zhou Baoyuan, and Li Yuting are each sentenced to one month of imprisonment and fined twenty yuan for smoking opium. Lu Arong, a repeat offender for smoking opium, is sentenced to four months of imprisonment and fined forty yuan; if the fine is not paid, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two yuan; the number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. A small can of opium ash, five opium pipes, six opium lamps, one opium tray, and two opium ledgers are to be confiscated. Wen Amao, Xia Shengrong, Xu Zuolong, Qian Arong, Tan Guangfu, and Fang Fugen are found not guilty.

41. Tao Baobao et al. v. Wang Fulin et al. for Suspicion of Embezzlement (Main Text): Wang Fulin, Wang Fugen, and Wang Maoda, accused of embezzlement, and Tao Baobao and Tao Ronghua, accused of false accusation and fraud, are all found not guilty; the related civil lawsuit is to be transferred to the civil court for adjudication.

Criminal Judgments

1. Li Caifu for Theft (Main Text): Li Caifu is sentenced to five months of imprisonment for theft; the number of days of detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

2. Wang Alin for Theft (Main Text): Wang Alin is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for theft during a disaster; the number of days of detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

3. Li Chen for Opium (Main Text): Li Chen is sentenced to six months of imprisonment and fined ninety yuan for the crime of transporting opium substitutes; if the fine is not paid through compulsory enforcement, it will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every one yuan; the number of days of detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment; red pills including the packaged boxes weighing a total of ninety taels, are to be confiscated and burned.

4. Wang Jinqing et al. for Obstructing Family (Main Text): Wang Jinqing and Su Xinyuan are each sentenced to one year of imprisonment for jointly enticing a woman under the age of twenty for the purpose of profit; the number of days of detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

Civil Judgments

1. Zhenhua Peppermint Factory v. Li Qianwan for a Case Involving Funds (Main Text): The defendant shall return to the plaintiff silver worth seven thousand taels, along with interest calculated at an annual rate of five percent from the date of the lawsuit until the date of the end of the execution; the defendant shall return the books and documents taken to the plaintiff; the private signing of agreements and unauthorized use of the plaintiff's seal shall be deemed invalid; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

2. Liu Agen et al. for Theft (Main Text): Liu Axian and Xu Linsheng are each sentenced to five months of imprisonment for joint theft; the number of days of detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

3. Wu Xiaocheng et al. for Fraud (Main Text): Wu Xiaocheng is sentenced to two months of imprisonment for jointly defrauding property; the number of days of detention will be credited at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment.

Shanghai Second Special District Local Court 152

Civil Judgments:

1. Sun Zhongzhao v. Yang Zuyong for Rent Arrears (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff rent of one thousand three hundred and three yuan and two jiao, and shall return the leased premises to the plaintiff; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. The first item of this judgment is approved for a declaration of provisional execution.

2. Dali v. Wu Dechang for Rent Arrears (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of six hundred and forty-four yuan; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

3. Zhu Huashun v. Xu Benliang for Goods Payment (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff forty-one yuan and four jiao; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant. This judgment shall be declared provisionally executable.

4. Zhou Baoqing v. Chen Jinfu for Goods Payment (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff one hundred yuan, five jiao, and three fen, along with interest at an annual rate of five percent from the date of the lawsuit until the date of the end of the execution; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

5. Song Hongsheng v. Pi Pao and Xu for Loan (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff seventy yuan; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

6. Li Chunqing v. Zhou Zhiting for Rent Arrears (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of four hundred and twenty-one yuan and five jiao; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

7. Jingye Company v. Wu for Rent Arrears (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of one hundred and eighty-four yuan; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

8. Taili Company v. Huixing Wood Company for Rent Arrears (Main Text): The defendant shall pay the plaintiff rent of two hundred and eighty taels of silver; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

9. Yuan Tai Zou Meisheng et al. v. Tiboike for Rent Arrears and Late Eviction Appeal Case (Main Text): The appeal is rejected; the second instance litigation costs shall be borne by the appellant.

10. Li Nuohuai v. Xu Gelin for Return of Equipment Case (Main Text): The defendant shall return all eight pieces of the plaintiff's equipment in their possession; if unable to return, the defendant shall compensate the plaintiff fifty yuan; the plaintiff's remaining claims are rejected; the litigation costs shall be borne by the defendant.

Civil Instructions

1. One case: Zhang Fujin's request for execution has been reviewed. As this case has already been instructed to have the claimant collect the funds at the court on April 8, the deadline was not followed. As the debtor Zhang Tingqing subsequently submitted two hundred yuan of the case funds, come to the court at 9:00 AM on the 25th of this month to collect them together without further delay. A separate date will be scheduled to summon the parties regarding the remaining amount owed. This instruction is hereby given.

2. One case: Chen Yuxiang's request to close the case has been reviewed. As it is stated that the case has been fundamentally resolved through mediation by relatives and friends, and a written agreement has been executed by both parties, the request to close the case is hereby approved. This instruction is hereby given.

3. One case: Zhu Boshilov's request to transfer management and issue a certificate has been reviewed. A vehicle of the debtor Melli Shequ has been seized and appraised by this court and a public notice for auction has been issued. However, as the period of the public notice has been long and there have been no buyers, the request to have the creditor manage the vehicle themselves and issue a certificate for the remaining amount owed is hereby approved. As there are ten yuan remaining from the twenty yuan of sealing fees previously paid, come to the court at 2:00 PM on the 27th of this month to collect it. This instruction is hereby given.

4. One case: Lu Jimei's renewed request for execution has been reviewed. As the movables of the debtor Wu Xijin had been seized by this court, the request to exempt the seizure because the value was insufficient to cover the claim was approved. As the request to seize the immovable property of the debtor has now been received, it is hereby approved. A date will be scheduled to notify the relevant officials to designate the area for sealing. This instruction is hereby given.

5. One case: Shanghai Commercial Savings Bank's renewed request for execution and collection of funds has been reviewed. As it is stated that the debtor Shagnorov's address has already changed, a date will be scheduled to summon the parties for execution. The ten yuan of sealing fees and the one hundred and twenty yuan of security deposit previously paid by the claimant shall be collected at the court at 2:00 PM on the 27th of this month. This instruction is hereby given.

6. One case: Wang Jingen et al.'s request to copy the mortgage certificate has been reviewed. After the order has copied the certificate, deliver it immediately. Gu Jirong's lawyer's announcement has been published. Please be advised that the announcement paper is attached to the file of the previous French Public Concession. This instruction is hereby given.

7. One case: Wang Gongxian's request to take over the management of the seized assets has been reviewed. The movable assets of the debtor Xie Chunsheng were seized and appraised by the court. The request by the creditor to take over the management of the assets is hereby approved as the value is roughly equivalent to the amount of the debt. A date will be scheduled to send an official to release the sealing and hand over the assets for management. Pay the execution fee of this case that has not been submitted. Be informed. This instruction is hereby given.
